[30;1m56 | [0m[35m    The transformer first finds the values at one or both tails of the distributions[0m
[30;1m57 | [0m[35m    (fit). The transformer then caps the variables (transform).[0m
[30;1m58 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m59 | [0m[35m    More details in the :ref:`User Guide <winsorizer>`.[0m

[30;1m37 | [0m[35m    MeanNormalizationScaler() applies mean normalization, which consists of subtracting[0m
